data-lemmaid=\"338801\">佘诗曼</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%8A/22585635\" data-lemmaid=\"22585635\">王菊</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E5%90%B4%E8%B0%A8%E8%A8%80/938739\" alt=\"活动倒计时2天海报——黄晓明\"\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t/>\n</a>\n</li>\n</ul>\n</div><button class=\"lemma-album-marquee__view__tool__btn lemma-album-marquee__view__tool__btn--left J-scrollleft\"><em class=\"cmn-icon cmn-icons cmn-icons_arrow-l-2\"></em></button>\n<button class=\"lemma-album-marquee__view__tool__btn lemma-album-marquee__view__tool__btn--right J-scrollright\"><em class=\"cmn-icon cmn-icons cmn-icons_arrow-r-2\"></em></button></div>\n<div class=\"lemma-album-marquee__desc\">\n活动倒计时海报\n</div>\n</div>\n</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00l4k\" ><b>时间：</b>2018.12.19-2019.2.9</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00l5v\" ><b>玩法：</b></div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00l7i\" ><b>（1）新年“星”祝福，明星祝你新年快乐</b></div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00l95\" >从线上80位明星中，选择你最中意的<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E6%98%8E%E6%98%9F/74\" data-lemmaid=\"74\">明星</a>，定制专属祝福视频，即可在<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%99%BE%E5%BA%A6/22343833\" data-lemmaid=\"22343833\">百度</a>App搜到“Ta对你的专属祝福”。</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00las\" >（2）我的爱豆我来宠，打榜赢情人节大屏幕<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E9%94%A6%E9%B2%A4/311179\" data-lemmaid=\"311179\">锦鲤</a></div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00lce\" >通过视频的观看、点赞、分享、使用，为爱豆增加热力值，热力值TOP3的明星，可获得<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%BA%B3%E6%96%AF%E8%BE%BE%E5%85%8B/17437\" data-lemmaid=\"17437\">纳斯达克</a>大屏幕、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%99%BE%E5%BA%A6%E7%99%BE%E7%A7%91/85895\" data-lemmaid=\"85895\">百度百科</a>App开屏等超强曝光资源。</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng00le0\" ><b>参与方式：</b>活动期间百度App搜索“秒懂本尊答”，即可找到活动入口。</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"tyPnTU4gGHzl\" ><b>听，文物在说话</b></div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng8sz3o\" ><b>主题：明星化身博物馆文物</b></div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"swZ6e8IMefGT\" ><b>内容：</b>联合<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%99%BE%E5%BA%A6%E7%99%BE%E7%A7%91%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%A6%86%E8%AE%A1%E5%88%92/22588438\" data-lemmaid=\"22588438\">百度百科博物馆计划</a>，与<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E5%A4%A7%E9%83%BD%E4%BC%9A%E8%89%BA%E6%9C%AF%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%A6%86/1292100\" data-lemmaid=\"1292100\">大都会艺术博物馆</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E5%A4%A7%E8%8B%B1%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%A6%86/490292\" data-lemmaid=\"490292\">大英博物馆</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%A7%A6%E5%A7%8B%E7%9A%87%E5%B8%9D%E9%99%B5%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%99%A2/6208743\" data-lemmaid=\"6208743\">秦始皇帝陵博物院</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E5%B1%B1%E8%A5%BF%E5%8D%9A%E7%89%A9%E9%A6%86/3913127\" data-lemmaid=\"3913127\">山西博物馆</a>等国外内知名博物馆合作，邀请明星以文物的第一视角，讲述文物的前世今生，并借助百度<a target=_blank href=\"/item/AR%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF/1496786\" data-lemmaid=\"1496786\">AR技术</a>，实现人与文物的完美结合。</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"gncng8sz5d\" >合作明星：<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E4%B8%A5%E5%B1%B9%E5%AE%BD/9794812\" data-lemmaid=\"9794812\">严屹宽</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E8%89%BE%E4%BC%A6/8146605\" data-lemmaid=\"8146605\">艾伦</a>、<a target=_blank ><b>100分自我介绍</b></div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"sTOAIXswWpKa\" >主题：明星介绍自己。</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"sTOANq8IJK4L\" >内容：明星大咖本尊出镜，以<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%80%E4%BA%BA%E7%A7%B0/9779234\" data-lemmaid=\"9779234\">第一人称</a>介绍自己的基础信息，如身高、体重、生日、家乡、毕业院校、代表作品等。同时，增加<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E5%BF%AB%E9%97%AE/4726511\" data-lemmaid=\"4726511\">快问</a>快答的环节，通过对日常生活、兴趣爱好、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E8%87%AA%E6%88%91%E8%AE%A4%E7%9F%A5/9480503\" data-lemmaid=\"9480503\">自我认知</a>等信息的深挖，为用户呈现一个更多维立体的本尊形象。《<a target=_blank href=\"/item/100%E5%88%86%E8%87%AA%E6%88%91%E4%BB%8B%E7%BB%8D/57723245\" data-lemmaid=\"57723245\">100分自我介绍</a>》<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E6%98%8E%E6%98%9F/19021348\" data-lemmaid=\"19021348\">作为明星</a>大咖的互联网名片之一，长期在本人百度<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%99%BE%E7%A7%91%E8%AF%8D%E6%9D%A1/1772433\" data-lemmaid=\"1772433\">百科词条</a>的首位展现。</div><div class=\"para MARK_MODULE\" label-module=\"para\" data-uuid=\"sTOARx5sL1ED\" >合作艺人：<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%8E%8B%E5%98%89%E5%B0%94/13002467\" data-lemmaid=\"13002467\">王嘉尔</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%8E%8B%E5%9C%A3%E8%BF%AA/9841762\" data-lemmaid=\"9841762\">王圣迪</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%8E%8B%E5%8B%89/23167224\" data-lemmaid=\"23167224\">王勉</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E6%9D%8E%E9%9D%99/20125276\" data-lemmaid=\"20125276\">李静</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E9%92%9F%E6%AC%A3%E6%BD%BC/9794318\" data-lemmaid=\"9794318\">钟欣潼</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E8%94%A1%E5%8D%93%E5%A6%8D/176132\" data-lemmaid=\"176132\">蔡卓妍</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E7%8E%8B%E5%AE%89%E5%AE%87/23640606\" data-lemmaid=\"23640606\">王安宇</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E5%96%BB%E6%81%A9%E6%B3%B0/193579\" data-lemmaid=\"193579\">喻恩泰</a>、<a target=_blank href=\"/item/%E9%9F%A9%E7%BE%8E%E5%A8%9F/23732381\" data-lemmaid=\"23732381\">韩美娟</a>等。</div><div
